// Hey, the code is pretty easy to understand, and if you plan to change anything here, remember that a reference to a treasure table starts with T_ and a reference to a specific item starts with I_
// If you want to add an item to a random loot lists, first put the item in a specific type(T_REL_Rarity_Type)
// then put the item in a general category(T_REL_All_Rarity)
// All of these loot lists are used in one way or another to transfer data to game locations.
// Paramonov
